<user>106322337117493005416<//user>< gmapID>
0x8085809d453be655:0xbbe8129adc4f786c< /gmapID>
<Pics>None<//Pics><Time>1393044511859<//Time><username>Erika Lam</username>< Text>
After a serious back injury in November 2013, my chiropractor insisted I get a new mattress to support my compromised spine, and so after visiting The Natural Mattress Store (very pricey but great), Keetsa (all synthetic memory foam that I'm allergic to), I stumbled upon Natural Sense showroom in SOMA looking for a natural foam latex mattress. It was a late Saturday evening and there were a bunch of other customers there, so my fiance and I got to lay on different mattresses without anyone hassling or talking to us at all.
After a while, Courtney began to help us, describing the differences in the numbers that shows the firmness of the mattresses and she was great about giving us the info without any sales-y schpeel. She was just very helpful, down to Earth and real. She even started to pull out different types of the mattress toppers on to the floor and was like "Try it out!". Lay on them on the floor. Very unpretentious.

The showroom is not as nice and fancy as other mattress places we'd been to (they don't offer you organic tea, or dimmers on the overhead lights while you lay down and take a nap). It's a little chilly and poorly lit, a little downtrodden, and a few homeless guys walked in while we were there, but what impressed me was how mellow the sales people were about the whole situation. Totally calm and respectful and asking "Can I help you?" That was cool. I like when people treat others kindly.

We ended up purchasing a Queen Natural Foam Latex mattress, with Extra Firm Layer on the bottom, Medium on the Top and all wrapped up in an organic cover with the wool topper. It was the end of the year so we got a 15% discount as well as 2 organic covered queen foam latex pillows.

Because of my back injury, I had been sleeping on a massage table camped out in my living room so I URGENTLY needed this mattress. I called in the next day to check on my order (it was New year's Eve) and Alan was so helpful and even though they were understaffed because of the holidays, he emailed me back to tell me that he had put a rush on my order to get my mattress cut and made for me.

I got a call when it was ready 5 days later and we went down to pick up the mattress, easily rolled up so it could fit in the back of my Toyota Camry. Super nice guys helped load it into my car and although the pillows didn't make it into my order, when I called later, they apologized and I picked them up after.

I've loved my mattress so much that when my 10 yo son complained that his back hurt because his bed was too hard, I ordered a twin latex foam mattress topper (Soft) to put on top of his ultra firm mattress and got a deal on the clearance site. His bed is now SO heavenly to lie on and he is sooooo happy!

I am now going to purchase a soft topper to put on my half of my firm queen mattress because it feels better on my bones (I'm only 100lbs) but my fiance wants to keep his half the same, so the Foam Order people said they would cut a twin mattress topper to fit just half of a queen sized bed. Nice!

Every time I've gone in/called/emailed the people at Foam Order, they have been so nice and helpful, always answering my multitude of questions with genuine concern and THAT kind of service is hard to find, so that's why I give them the 5 stars. And I LOVE THESE MATTRESSES! Comfy. No Smell (I"m allergic to most mattresses smells and especially the memory foam!)

Great people. Great prices. Great product.<//Text>

< Review>
I've been living at the Villa del Cerro apartment complex for 5 years now, and before Jensen took over it was pretty rocky. The previous company was shady and wouldn't get anything done in a reasonably timely manner. As soon as Jensen replaced that company, things here have gotten much better. The work order response time still pleasantly surprises me, as I know the maintenance men will do their best to complete fixes as soon as they can. Not once since Jensen have we been charged for replacement of electrical fixes that were simply outdated (e.g. the 2 prong outlets, kitchen and bathroom bulbs, etc). And I truly appreciate Peter Brunetto for his management of this property. He really listens and does his best to address any issues that have come up since his arrival here. He has by far done THE most than any other manager has (prior to Jensen's management). Slowly but surely, Jensen is doing their best to update the physical property and make it better for tenants and visitors alike.</Review>

<user>110411355602439781931< /user><GmapID>0x80e81901ad46a4c7:0x8a9150c2df9e69d2</GmapID>< Review>
We had ordered a full pack and move on the kitchen and two children's rooms, plus moving of all the major furniture.  The packers were supposed to pack for three hours but only stayed for two and a half. They did not finish packing up one of the kids' rooms.  The next day, the movers moved everything that had been packed, the furniture, and boxes from the garage, but did not include all the loose items in the kids' rooms.

The movers themselves were great. They were courteous, hard working, and dedicated to getting the job done. But I am disappointed that we did not get the service that we signed up (and paid) for. We had to take several trips by car to retrieve the items left behind in the room that was supposed to be fully packed and moved.

Bottom line: I would hire Meathead again in a flash, but I would be careful to put better safeguards into the contract to ensure that all agreed-upon items are in fact moved.</Review>

A downright dirty and dishonest business...!!

Meathead Movers damaged 200 square feet of hardwood flooring in a rental my family moved out of. We eyewitnessed a crew member dragging a heavy item across the floor and doing the damage, then proceeded to confront the crew immediately to get the damage documented right away. Everyone was on the same page and they promised they would take responsibility, so we felt they were a professional operation up to that point.

When we got the bill for the repair from our landlord (more than $3000 out of our security deposit!!) and sent it to Meathead Movers for reimbursement, they changed their story completely and denied having damaged the floor at all. After their so-called "internal investigation" we were served with a "final resolution" letter which said the crew did not do the damage, they had no incentive to lie, there was no way for that damage to have occurred, so it was evident that they were not liable. All of which were just lies upon lies.

For all the positive reviews they get they sure don't step up and do the right thing when it counts the most!

Stay far, far away and hire someone else for your move.< /review>

My sister is a huge fan of this place. She loves indian authentic food. Her office colleagues too have become addicted to the butter chicken,  saag paneer, the dum biryaniz from this place. I personally feel they have a great menu soc the top selling items , tandoor menu and the flavours are really very unique .
Veg platter, non  veg platter with salad its quiet filling. I feel rather than having a huge menu with chinese n other items and not delivering quality and taste, its better to have a menu one can cater with authentic taste, quality and consistency.  Their mutton biryani is way more better than any other restaurants i have tried till date. The fish tikka and chicken seekh kebab are worth ordering for parties and family occasions .
They had catered once for my sisters party and people loved the food. The pricing is very much cheaper compared to restaurants in mountain view area. This place is underrated i feel for the quality and tasteful food they cater. I would highly recommend this place and encourage people to write reviews which would help people rely on before they order.</Text>

The food here is really delicious ...i would give4/5 for the curry items.. the best part is it does not give one heavy stuff feeling ..less of oil and feels fresh and healthy.
The tandoor items wld be 5/5 since the meat is always fresh juicy and lots of salad that comes along...its as good as whole meal in itself.
Biryanis all wld be 4/5 very much authentic..well spiced and best quality rice which i dint observe any other indian restaurant as of now .

< Review>
Recent Visit2
I'm surprised by the way this restaurant has improved, compared to my previous visit, many months ago. I have noticed that they were getting many takeout orders.

I have ordered Hyderabadi chicken dum biryani. The service was on time. It took around 15 min for my order to arrive.
Biryani was very delicious. Perfectly cooked chicken, along with boiled egg, in a flavorful basmati rice. Gravy and raitha were also delicious..!!
Everything was so close to "authentic hyderabadi biryani" that I decided to write an updated review on yelp.

Only thing is, if they can improve the service in handling customers a little bit, this will be an awesome restaurant.

P.S. This review is only for the Hyderabadi chicken dum biryani. I will   definitely try other biryanis from this restaurant soon..!

Visit1
I decided to try this restaurant after seeing the name biryaniz and their tag line "asli biryani" (meaning original biryani). Went here for dinner on Tue.

Another crappy Indian restaurant just like many others in the south bay.
1) Unorganized. No one to seat you/ explain you/ to give the menu. You might feel other customers requesting you to move ( or touching) while eating because the tables are so close to each other that they can't leave until you move your chair forward.
2) Very slow. By the time you get your biryani your hunger will be dead. It took more than 30 min to get my order.
3) Bad service. Only 1 waiter trying to do everything. You have to keep asking the waiter again and again. Not just myself, there were other customers too requesting the waiter repeatedly that they didn't get their order served completely.
4) Flavorless Biryani. I still tried to be patient hoping the chicken dum biryani will be good but it is just bland biryani with too much rice and 2 chicken pieces and 1 egg.
mirchi ka saalan (gravy that comes with biryani) is all watery.
raita was ok.

P.S. This is Nakli biryani( meaning fake biryani). No way nearer to asli biryani as they claim. Another crappy biryani joint. Attached photos supporting my review.</Review>

<userid>105146863913853623373< /userid>< username>
Sheryl Houston</username>
<date>1578321402812<//date><rating>5< /rating>< text>
My husband and I walked into this restaurant on a whim with our 4 month old son. It was later at night and the staff greeted us with friendly smiles. They were running low on some of their staples but they eagerly talked us through the menu which helped us out a lot. I ordered a very spicy dish (I really like spicy food) and the man taking our order kindly let me know that their food is extra spicy compared to other local cuisines. He was right! I got the medium spice level and it was very spicy. I think they could tell I was having a bit of a tough time because they offered me extra raita sauce and a mango lassi. I couldn't believe how kind and friendly the service was. Not only that, but even though the dish was extremely spicy it was so delicious. It was worth every bite. I ordered a small and it was enough food for 3 meals and all for 14 dollars! The food was so fresh, and the service was above and beyond. Our 4 month old son started crying so we had to leave quickly after starting to eat, but the staff was super kind about it and gave us a carry out bag with extra sauces. I would say this is a great casual eating spot with incredible food and a relaxed family atmosphere. It was easy for us to wheel in our son's stroller. Their ordering process is very efficient too. You order at the register and they give you a number that you take to any table you want to sit at. Our food also came out relatively quickly. I'm so happy that this place is on Castro. It's a step above the other restaurants and half the price for the amount of food you get. I can't wait to go again!</text>

<userid>114714540192669718999</userid><pictures>None<//pictures>< date>
1518499908405< /date>
<Response>None<//Response><review>Ordered the spicy shrimp biryani and fish biryani here.

The space is warm in feel and clean. Service is great, they really do go out of their way to ensure a welcoming experience.

The large portion of biryani truly is large; bring a second person or a big appetite. The basmati is light and fluffy, absorbs the yogurt and spicy flavors well. Do be warned that when you order spicy, it is indeed spicy. There is no playing around with the spices here. The flavors are intense and linger after the meal is over.

Between the fish and the shrimp, I'd recommend the fish. The meat and spicy sauce are at the base of the dish and it's up to the user's to make the rice as spicy as they'd like. This, however, means the protein can come out overcooked by the steam and heat. The shrimp can get a bit tough if you leave them there. The fish handles the heat much better.< /review>< Rating>
4<//Rating>

< review>
I had a really good experience coming to this restaurant. The food was excellent, especially the Hyderabadi Chicken Dum Biriyani and Chicken Tikka Kabab. The staff was courteous and attentive, though you may need to get used to the token system - which gets overly compensated with the food quality at such a low price.
I read few comments dinging them about service but based on my experience seems like they have resolve them.
To sum it up - if you are interested in authentic Indian food with good service, then this is the place to be. I highly recommend them!</review>

Biryaniz - Mountain View is the most authentic Biriyani place. Their Hyderabadi Goat Biryani and Lamb Keema Biryani are my favorite. Their biriyani's are delicious and authentic. They have surprises in the menu. I tasted different flavors in different items here unlike many Indian Restaurants around here where every items tastes same.

I have had "so called" biriyani in many places around here and in USA. I wish they knew what they are selling as Biriyani is nothing but meet-rice mix. People, who are not really familiar with our food taste and food culture, can be easily fooled with such Biriyani.
